### 387. Collaborative Argumentation for Learning

Type: report | Source: Digital Promise
Tags: k-12, formative-assessment, digital-promise
URL: https://digitalpromise.dspacedirect.org/items/6e1127b0-a7c6-4dc0-9769-c8f3c5100b63

This primer explores the benefits and challenges of integrating collaborative argumentation practices into classrooms to deepen student understanding and foster critical thinking, identifying argumentation as a key approach for building scientific knowledge and improving content learning. The document outlines strategies for supporting students' argumentation skills, fostering a culture of critical communication, and overcoming obstacles such as time constraints and lack of systemic support. Recommendations include introducing argumentation as knowledge building and consensus, establishing a classroom culture of respect and curiosity, incorporating multiple perspectives, and creating authentic opportunities for in-depth argumentation.

### 388. Assessment During Collaborative Learning

Type: report | Source: Digital Promise
Tags: k-12, formative-assessment, digital-promise
URL: https://digitalpromise.dspacedirect.org/items/8c0a25a2-0a7a-4ebb-be02-49a82e61e726

This primer explores assessment during collaborative learning, shifting focus from traditional summative evaluation to ongoing formative assessment, and addresses key questions about what should be assessed—individual knowledge, group dynamics, collaborative skills, or some combination. The document outlines effective practices for incorporating self- and peer-assessment to empower students, provides guidance on delivering meaningful feedback, and discusses balancing individual and group assessments to ensure students learn content and collaborate successfully. It offers practical strategies, example assessments, and research-based insights to facilitate application of these principles in classroom settings.

### 389. Classroom Discourse

Type: report | Source: Digital Promise
Tags: k-12, formative-assessment, sel, digital-promise
URL: https://digitalpromise.dspacedirect.org/items/8c56887b-c699-4999-8711-53fad39077bd

This primer explores student-centered classroom discourse, examining its benefits and challenges and providing strategies for effective implementation, emphasizing a shift from traditional "Initiation-Response-Evaluation" patterns to interactive approaches that enhance engagement, deeper processing, reasoning skills, and active listening. The document discusses methods such as "accountable talk" and "exploratory talk," highlights the crucial role of teachers in modeling effective talk moves and setting clear expectations, and addresses challenges such as unequal participation and power dynamics. Practical strategies include establishing ground rules, planning thought-provoking questions, using diverse talk formats, and incorporating talk moves to foster productive classroom discussions.

### 390. Voices of Undergraduate Students Taking Introductory Statistics Courses

Type: report | Source: Digital Promise
Tags: higher-ed, digital-learning-platforms, formative-assessment, student-belonging, digital-promise
URL: https://digitalpromise.dspacedirect.org/items/f0b7d6ee-9140-4241-8ce3-1474fd42b74e

This report presents findings from a 2023–24 study by Achieving the Dream examining the experiences of 50 undergraduate students in introductory statistics courses using Lumen One courseware, highlighting the effectiveness of courseware features providing formative practice with feedback. The study explores how instructor involvement and course modality influence student engagement and sense of belonging, particularly among students of color, finding that about half of students indicated their instructors assisted them in connecting courseware content to their understanding. Recommendations emphasize improving feedback mechanisms and increasing instructor engagement to better support student success, while also noting that students appreciated real-world examples and low-stakes assessments.

### 387. NAEP — The Nation's Report Card

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, formative-assessment, longitudinal
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/nationsreportcard/

The Nation's Report Card (NAEP) is the largest nationally representative and continuing assessment of what America's students know and can do across subjects including mathematics, reading, science, civics, and others. It provides a common measure of student achievement that offers a window into the state of the K-12 education system, with results reported at national, state, and district levels. Data tools allow users to explore NAEP results, access assessment items, and download datasets for research.

---

### 388. IPEDS — Integrated Postsecondary Education Data System

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: higher-ed, open-datasets, longitudinal, data-sharing
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/ipeds/

IPEDS is the primary source for data on U.S. colleges, universities, and technical and vocational institutions, consisting of 12 interrelated survey components conducted annually that gather data from every institution participating in federal student financial aid programs. Data collections cover enrollment, completions, graduation rates, finance, human resources, student financial aid, and more, with releases each fall, winter, and spring. Users can access institutional data through interactive tools, create custom analyses, or download full survey datasets for research.

---

### 389. Common Core of Data (CCD)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, data-sharing
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/ccd/aboutCCD.asp

The Common Core of Data (CCD) is the Department of Education's primary database on public elementary and secondary education in the United States, comprising a comprehensive annual national database of all public elementary and secondary schools and school districts. CCD collects nonfiscal data through the EDFacts office and fiscal data separately, with publications covering school directories, dropout and graduation rates, district finances, and enrollment. Researchers can search the bibliography for articles, books, and dissertations based on CCD data, and use the EDFIN tool for public school finance information.

---

### 390. Early Childhood Longitudinal Study (ECLS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: early-childhood, open-datasets, longitudinal, prekindergarten
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/ecls/

The Early Childhood Longitudinal Study (ECLS) program provides information about children's knowledge, skills, and development from birth through elementary school, comprising four longitudinal studies that examine child development, school readiness, and early school experiences. Studies include a birth cohort (ECLS-B) following children born in 2001, the kindergarten classes of 1998–99 and 2010–11, and the newest ECLS-K:2024 following the kindergarten class of 2023–24 through third grade. The program provides data to analyze relationships among family, school, community, and individual factors with children's development and early learning.

---

### 391. High School Longitudinal Study of 2009 (HSLS:09)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, longitudinal, career-readiness, college-access, math-education
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/hsls09/

HSLS:09 is a nationally representative longitudinal study of more than 23,000 9th graders from 944 schools in 2009, with follow-ups in 2012 and 2016 and postsecondary administrative records through 2021. The study includes surveys of students, parents, math and science teachers, school administrators, and counselors, along with a student assessment in algebraic skills, reasoning, and problem solving. Data collection waves span from the 2009 base year through postsecondary transcripts, enabling research on transitions from high school into college and the workforce, including 10 state-representative datasets.

---

### 392. Education Longitudinal Study of 2002 (ELS:2002)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, longitudinal, college-access
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/els2002/

ELS:2002 is a nationally representative longitudinal study of 10th graders in 2002, following students through secondary and postsecondary years with data collection waves spanning from the 2002 base year through a 2012 third follow-up and 2013 postsecondary transcripts. The study focuses on students' trajectories from high school into postsecondary education, the workforce, and beyond, including patterns of college access and persistence, with surveys of students, parents, math and English teachers, and school administrators. High school transcripts and postsecondary transcripts are available for research on coursetaking and grades; public-use data are accessible through the NCES DataLab.

---

### 393. National Education Longitudinal Study of 1988 (NELS:88)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, longitudinal, college-access, career-readiness
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/nels88/

NELS:88 is a nationally representative longitudinal study of 8th graders in 1988, following students through secondary and postsecondary years across four follow-ups through 2000, 12 years after the baseline survey. The study collected surveys from students on school, work, and home experiences, educational aspirations, and peer and parent influences, along with student assessments in reading, social studies, mathematics, and science at 8th, 10th, and 12th grades. High school and postsecondary transcript data are available, and the study was designed to provide trend data on critical transitions from middle school through postsecondary education and the labor force.

---

### 394. Beginning Postsecondary Students Longitudinal Study (BPS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: higher-ed, open-datasets, longitudinal, college-access, dropout-prevention
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/bps/

The Beginning Postsecondary Students (BPS) Longitudinal Study surveys cohorts of first-time beginning students at three points: at the end of their first year, and three and six years after first starting postsecondary education. Cohorts are drawn from the National Postsecondary Student Aid Study (NPSAS), with the most recent completed study (BPS:12/17) containing data on approximately 22,500 students and the current cohort (BPS:20/22) representing approximately 3.3 million undergraduates who first enrolled in 2019–20. Data track students' paths through postsecondary education and address policy questions about completion, financial aid, and credential attainment.

---

### 395. Civil Rights Data Collection (CRDC)

Type: dataset | Source: U.S. Department of Education Office for Civil Rights
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, school-discipline, english-learners, data-sharing
URL: https://civilrightsdata.ed.gov/about

The Civil Rights Data Collection (CRDC) has collected civil rights data related to students' access and barriers to educational opportunity from early childhood through grade 12 since 1968, and since the 2011–12 collection has been administered every two years to all public school districts and schools in the 50 states and Washington, D.C. The CRDC collects information on student enrollment, access to courses, programs, and school staff, and school climate factors such as bullying, harassment, and student discipline, with most data disaggregated by race, ethnicity, sex, disability, and English Learner status. It is a key enforcement tool under civil rights laws prohibiting discrimination based on race, color, national origin, sex, disability, and age.

---

### 396. Urban Institute Education Data Explorer

Type: dataset | Source: Urban Institute
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, open-datasets, data-sharing
URL: https://educationdata.urban.org/

The Urban Institute's Education Data Explorer aggregates data from multiple federal and other education sources into a single platform, allowing users to build custom datasets by narrowing by education level, geography, timeframe, and indicator. The tool is designed to make it easier to generate rigorous, accurate, and actionable insights to improve student outcomes, with access available through an interactive explorer or a full API for programmatic use. The platform is oriented toward evidence-based policy decisions and is freely accessible under published terms of use.

---

### 397. National Student Clearinghouse Research Center

Type: dataset | Source: National Student Clearinghouse
Tags: higher-ed, open-datasets, college-access, longitudinal, dropout-prevention
URL: https://nscresearchcenter.org/

The National Student Clearinghouse Research Center publishes relevant, objective data on postsecondary metrics using enrollment and completion records from the majority of U.S. institutions, with publication series covering undergraduate degree earners, transfer outcomes, enrollment trends, persistence and retention, and high school benchmark data. Reports track cohort outcomes longitudinally—for example, reporting that the national 6-year college completion rate for fall 2019 starters was 61.1%—and provide comparisons by student demographics, institution type, and state. Data and reports guide policymakers and institutional leaders on issues of college access, transfer, and completion.

---

### 398. PISA — Programme for International Student Assessment (Data)

Type: dataset | Source: OECD
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, longitudinal, math-education, literacy
URL: https://www.oecd.org/pisa/data/

The PISA database contains the full set of responses from individual students, school principals, and parents, available for download in SPSS and SAS formats across assessment cycles from 2000 to 2022. Designed for statisticians and professional researchers, the files include background questionnaires, codebooks, and compendia alongside analytical tools such as the PISA Education GPS for downloading full indicator sets and generating country profile reports. The OECD also provides the PISA Data Analysis Manual and IEA IDB Analyzer software to support accurate use of the complex survey methodology.

---

### 399. TIMSS — Trends in International Mathematics and Science Study (Databases)

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, math-education
URL: https://timssandpirls.bc.edu/databases-landing.html

The TIMSS and PIRLS International Databases are publicly available to researchers, analysts, and anyone interested in improving education, with the aim of supporting broad use of the data. The databases include student mathematics, science, and reading achievement data as well as student, parent, teacher, school, and curricular background data for all participating countries across multiple assessment cycles. A public use version of the datasets is available for download, covering TIMSS cycles from 1995 through 2023 and TIMSS Advanced assessments.

---

### 400. PIRLS 2021 — Progress in International Reading Literacy Study (International Database)

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, literacy
URL: https://timssandpirls.bc.edu/pirls2021/international-database/

The PIRLS 2021 International Database includes student reading achievement data and student, home, teacher, school, and national context data for 57 countries and 8 benchmarking participants, representing the fifth PIRLS cycle since 2001 and 20 years of trend data at the fourth grade. Because data collection occurred during COVID-19 school disruptions, the database provides a uniquely rich source for researching pandemic impacts on teaching and learning reading. Data are available in R, SPSS, and SAS formats along with codebooks, item parameters, almanacs, and analysis programs; a restricted-use version is also available through the IEA Study Data Repository for variables removed from the public release.

---

### 401. World Bank EdStats — Education Statistics Portal

Type: dataset | Source: World Bank
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, open-datasets
URL: https://datatopics.worldbank.org/education/

The World Bank EdStats Portal provides easy access to key education indicators spanning access, completion, learning outcomes, expenditures, policy, and equity from pre-primary through tertiary levels. In addition to the core EdStats database, the portal links to specialized datasets including the Learning Poverty database, the Harmonized Learning Outcomes database, and Country Learning Outcomes (CLO) of harmonized learning assessments. The portal is currently being revamped to improve user experience and relevance, with all datasets remaining accessible via direct download links during the transition.

---

### 402. ICPSR — Education Research Studies

Type: dataset | Source: ICPSR (U. Michigan)
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, open-datasets, data-sharing
URL: https://www.icpsr.umich.edu/web/ICPSR/search/studies?q=education&ARCHIVE=ICPSR&PUBLISH_STATUS=PUBLISHED

ICPSR's searchable archive contains over 11,000 published education-related studies, spanning topics from early childhood and K-12 schooling to higher education finance, adult education, and special education. Studies are contributed by investigators across government agencies and universities and are available with associated variables (87,000+), series (309), and data-related publications (7,800+). The archive supports filtering by subject terms, geography, restriction type, data format, collection method, and funding agency, enabling targeted access to replication data and primary survey datasets.

---

### 403. Opportunity Insights — Education and Mobility Data Library

Type: dataset | Source: Harvard University
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, open-datasets, longitudinal, college-access
URL: https://opportunityinsights.org/data/

Opportunity Insights publishes a publicly available data library of datasets produced alongside its research studies, enabling other researchers and practitioners to analyze social mobility, education, life expectancy, patent rates, and other outcomes by neighborhood, college, parental income level, and racial background. Datasets are provided in CSV and Stata formats with codebooks and replication code, and cover topics including college-level data for 139 selective American colleges, social capital by county, student loan balances, and cohort-level trends in outcomes from 1978 to 1992 birth cohorts. Users can filter the library by geographic level, topic, and paper title, and contact the team for technical assistance.

---

### 404. Stanford Education Data Archive (SEDA)

Type: dataset | Source: Stanford CEPA
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, longitudinal, math-education
URL: https://cepa.stanford.edu/seda/overview

The Stanford Education Data Archive, produced by the Educational Opportunity Project at Stanford University, is the first national database of academic performance measuring educational opportunity in every community in America across reading and math. The archive supports three active projects — the 2009-2019 Educational Opportunity Project (updated February 2026 with new trend data), the Education Recovery Project tracking learning loss and pandemic recovery across districts, and the Segregation Tracking Project mapping school and neighborhood segregation over decades. Data, interactive explorers, and research papers are freely available, with the most recent update adding new opportunity, recovery, and segregation data.

---

### 405. PSLC DataShop KDD Cup 2010 Educational Data Mining Challenge

Type: dataset | Source: Carnegie Mellon University LearnLab
Tags: learning-engineering, open-datasets, k-12, math-education, intelligent-tutoring, cmu-learnlab
URL: https://pslcdatashop.web.cmu.edu/KDDCup/

The KDD Cup 2010 challenge asked participants to predict student performance on mathematical problems from logs of student interaction with Intelligent Tutoring Systems, using five datasets (three development, two challenge) drawn from real ITS interactions. The task explored how generally or narrowly students learn, how quickly they improve, and whether knowledge requirements of problems can be inferred directly from student performance data. Post-competition submissions and a leaderboard remain available for continued benchmarking.

---

### 406. LearnSphere — Education Research Data Infrastructure

Type: dataset | Source: Carnegie Mellon University LearnLab
Tags: learning-engineering, open-datasets, data-sharing, cmu-learnlab
URL: https://learnsphere.org/

LearnSphere integrates existing and new educational data and analysis repositories to offer what it describes as the world's largest learning analytics infrastructure, combining linked data, analysis methods, and portal access to resources including DataShop, MOOCdb, DiscourseDB, and DataStage. The platform's Tigris workflow authoring tool facilitates the creation and sharing of custom analyses across multiple institutions including CMU, Memphis, Stanford, and ALTTAI. LearnSphere supports data-driven course design and large-scale distributed data infrastructure for education researchers.

---

### 407. Open University Learning Analytics Dataset (OULAD)

Type: dataset | Source: The Open University
Tags: learning-engineering, open-datasets, higher-ed, digital-learning-platforms, longitudinal
URL: https://analyse.kmi.open.ac.uk/

The Open University Learning Analytics Dataset (OULAD) contains anonymised data about courses, students, and their interactions with the Virtual Learning Environment (VLE) for seven selected Open University modules, with course presentations marked by start month. The dataset consists of tables stored in CSV format connected via unique identifiers, covering student demographic data and fine-grained VLE activity logs. OULAD has been used in learning analytics hackathons at multiple international conferences and received the Educational Dataset Prize from the Educational Data Mining Society in 2023.

---

### 408. ASSISTments Dataset

Type: dataset | Source: Worcester Polytechnic Institute
Tags: learning-engineering, open-datasets, k-12, math-education, intelligent-tutoring, formative-assessment, assistments
URL: https://sites.google.com/site/assistmentsdata/

The ASSISTments data repository hosts multiple publicly released datasets from the ASSISTments intelligent tutoring platform, covering student interactions, skill builder sequences, affect data, and log files from various research studies published from 2009 onward. All datasets are scrubbed of personally identifiable information and released under IRB-approved terms of use; researchers who discover residual PII are required to report and delete it. The project reflects a commitment to open science, requiring graduate students to release anonymized data and code alongside each published paper.

---

### 409. EdNet — Large-Scale Hierarchical Dataset in Education

Type: dataset | Source: Riiid
Tags: learning-engineering, open-datasets, k-12, intelligent-tutoring, digital-learning-platforms
URL: https://github.com/riiid/ednet

EdNet is a large-scale dataset of student-system interactions collected over two years by Santa, a multi-platform AI tutoring service with more than 780,000 users in Korea, comprising 131 million interactions from 784,309 students across iOS, Android, and web platforms. The dataset records diverse student actions — including which learning materials were consumed, responses, time spent, and lecture-watching — organized into a four-level hierarchy (KT1 through KT4) of increasing interaction richness. EdNet is described as the largest publicly available education dataset in terms of total students, interactions, and interaction types, and is accompanied by a published paper (arXiv:1912.03072) and an open leaderboard.

---

### 410. Duolingo Shared Task on Second Language Acquisition Modeling (SLAM)

Type: dataset | Source: Duolingo
Tags: learning-engineering, open-datasets, english-learners, nlp, longitudinal, duolingo
URL: https://sharedtask.duolingo.com/2018.html

The 2018 Duolingo Shared Task on Second Language Acquisition Modeling (SLAM) provided participating teams with transcripts from millions of exercises completed by thousands of Duolingo learners over their first 30 days of study, annotated at the token level for mistakes, with the task of predicting future learner errors. Three tracks covered learners of English, Spanish, and French, enabling research into personalized adaptive SLA modeling and language forgetting over time; 15 teams participated and the best systems improved upon a logistic regression baseline by 12%. The task was conducted in conjunction with the 13th BEA Workshop and NAACL-HLT 2018.

---

### 411. NBER Education Research Data

Type: dataset | Source: NBER
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, open-datasets, longitudinal
URL: https://www.nber.org/research/data?page=1&perPage=50&q=education

The NBER Public Use Data Archive is a repository of public-use economic, demographic, and enterprise datasets assembled to support NBER-affiliated researchers, including datasets relevant to education such as school district data, birth and natality records, and population survey files. Files are often reformatted for research convenience relative to original sources, and the archive also hosts data and code outputs from NBER research projects intended for replication. Researchers can request that the NBER host data or code from NBER-associated papers, projects, or grants via a formal submission process.

---

### 412. TALIS — Teaching and Learning International Survey

Type: dataset | Source: OECD
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, professional-development, longitudinal
URL: https://www.oecd.org/education/talis/

TALIS is the world's largest international survey about teachers and school leaders. Since 2008, it has gathered information from teachers and school leaders about working conditions and learning environments in over 60 education systems. TALIS 2024 sampled approximately 280,000 teachers in 17,000 schools across 55 education systems. The survey covers ISCED 2 teachers and school leaders, with additional modules for ISCED 1 and ISCED 3, as well as a Teacher Knowledge Survey (TKS) module. A companion survey, TALIS Starting Strong, focuses on early childhood staff and centre leaders. Results are used by policymakers to improve teaching and learning around the world; the next cycle is planned for 2030.

---

### 413. PIAAC — Programme for the International Assessment of Adult Competencies

Type: dataset | Source: OECD
Tags: higher-ed, open-datasets, longitudinal
URL: https://www.oecd.org/skills/piaac/

PIAAC is a programme of assessment and analysis of adult skills whose major product is the Survey of Adult Skills — an international computer-based household survey of adults aged 16–65, designed as 10-yearly cycles. The survey measures adults' proficiency in literacy, numeracy, and problem solving, and collects data on how adults use these skills at home and at work. The 1st Cycle was conducted in three rounds between 2011 and 2018 across 39 countries, interviewing approximately 245,000 adults representing 1.15 billion people. A 2nd Cycle covering 31 countries and economies completed its first round of data collection in 2022–2023, with results released in December 2024. Data support evidence-based decisions in workforce development, lifelong learning, and social inclusion.

---

### 414. National Teacher and Principal Survey (NTPS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, professional-development
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/ntps/

The National Teacher and Principal Survey (NTPS) is a system of related questionnaires that provides descriptive data on the context of public and private elementary and secondary education in the United States. Redesigned from the Schools and Staffing Survey (SASS), NTPS collects information directly from teachers and principals to provide local, state, and national policymakers with statistics on the condition of education. The survey supports analysis of principal, teacher, and student characteristics in detail and enables subgroup analysis (e.g., by gender, race/ethnicity, school locale). Paired with Teacher Follow-up Surveys (TFS) and Principal Follow-up Surveys (PFS), NTPS tracks teacher and principal attrition and mobility. The most recent main collection covered 2020–21, with follow-up surveys in 2021–22.

---

### 415. National Household Education Surveys Program (NHES)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, early-childhood, open-datasets, longitudinal
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/nhes/

The National Household Education Surveys Program (NHES) is the flagship household survey program of the National Center for Education Statistics (NCES). It collects nationally representative, descriptive data on the educational activities of children and families in the United States. Surveys are conducted every three to four years on rotating topics; current focus areas include early childhood care and education, parent and family involvement in schools, and homeschooling. Data enable trend analysis over time. The most recent administration concluded in August 2023, with reports released in September 2024 covering early childhood program participation and parent and family involvement in education.

---

### 416. EDFacts Data Files

Type: dataset | Source: U.S. Department of Education
Tags: k-12, open-datasets, data-sharing
URL: https://www2.ed.gov/about/inits/ed/edfacts/index.html

EDFacts is a U.S. Department of Education initiative to collect, analyze, and promote the use of high-quality pre-kindergarten through grade 12 data. It centralizes data provided by state education agencies (SEAs), including district and school demographics, program participation, and performance data. EDFacts integrates SEA-supplied performance data with other departmental data assets (such as financial grant information) to support planning, policymaking, and budget decision-making at federal, state, and local levels. The initiative aims to place robust, timely performance data at the core of education decision-making, reduce state and district data reporting burden, and improve state data capabilities through technical assistance.

---

### 417. National Assessment of Adult Literacy (NAAL)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: literacy, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/naal/

The National Assessment of Adult Literacy (NAAL) is a comprehensive national assessment measuring English language literacy skills among American adults aged 16 and older, representing the nation's most comprehensive measure of adult literacy since the 1992 National Adult Literacy Survey. The 2003 survey involved over 19,000 participants across all 50 states and D.C., plus approximately 1,200 incarcerated individuals in federal and state prisons. The assessment covers reading proficiency, health literacy, and background characteristics, providing demographic breakdowns that connect socioeconomic factors to literacy outcomes for researchers, policymakers, and practitioners.

---

### 418. Beginning Teacher Longitudinal Study (BTLS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, longitudinal, professional-development, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/btls/

The Beginning Teacher Longitudinal Study (BTLS) followed a nationally representative cohort of beginning public school teachers first interviewed during the 2007–08 Schools and Staffing Survey through the 2011–12 school year. Unlike typical teacher surveys that provide only a momentary snapshot, BTLS tracked the same cohort over five years to examine career development, attrition, and retention patterns. The study collected data on base salaries, certificate renewals, content area additions, and participation in leadership activities, providing a longitudinal view of early-career teacher trajectories.

---

### 419. Career and Technical Education Statistics (CTE Stats)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, career-readiness, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/ctes/

The Career and Technical Education (CTE) Statistics program delivers comprehensive national data on CTE participation and outcomes from high school through adult and postsecondary education, examining student enrollment patterns, teacher workforce characteristics, and coursetaking by student demographics. The program tracks CTE concentrators across secondary, postsecondary subbaccalaureate, and adult credential programs, and compares their educational trajectories against non-concentrators. Findings from the 2013 high school graduate cohort show CTE concentrators were more likely to earn associate's degrees but less likely to earn bachelor's degrees compared to peers.

---

### 420. Middle Grades Longitudinal Study of 2017–18 (MGLS:2017)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, longitudinal, formative-assessment, sel, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/mgls/

The Middle Grades Longitudinal Study of 2017–18 (MGLS:2017) tracked a nationally representative sample of approximately 13,300 sixth-graders across 570 schools to examine the academic, social-emotional, and environmental factors shaping student success and high school readiness during the middle grades transition. Data were collected from five respondent types—students, parents, teachers, special education staff, and school administrators—covering mathematics and reading assessments, executive function, family involvement, and school context. Two collection waves (spring 2018 and spring 2020) followed students through eighth grade, with the second wave shifting to remote participation due to the COVID-19 pandemic; restricted-use files are available to licensed researchers.

---

### 421. School Pulse Panel (SPP)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, attendance, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/spp/

The School Pulse Panel (SPP) surveys a nationally representative sample of public K-12 schools on high-priority education topics once a month during the school year, providing near-real-time data on school operations and student outcomes. The program collects information on student attendance rates, academic readiness, tutoring availability, and other operational metrics, with interactive results organized by topic, geography, and school characteristics. Recent findings (June 2025) indicate that 31% of students were reported as behind grade level, 85% of schools offered tutoring services, and the average daily attendance rate was 91%.

---

### 422. National Postsecondary Student Aid Study (NPSAS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: higher-ed, college-access, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/npsas/

The National Postsecondary Student Aid Study (NPSAS) examines the characteristics of students enrolled in postsecondary education with a special focus on how they finance their education, integrating student surveys, institutional records, and government administrative data. Conducted every three to four years since 1987, the study covers nationally representative samples of undergraduate and graduate students across all 50 states, D.C., and Puerto Rico. Recent 2019–20 findings show that 72% of undergraduates received financial aid averaging $14,100, while 74% of graduate students received aid averaging $25,300; the study also serves as the sampling frame for NCES longitudinal follow-up studies.

---

### 423. Baccalaureate and Beyond Longitudinal Study (B&B)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: higher-ed, longitudinal, career-readiness, college-access, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/b&b/

The Baccalaureate and Beyond Longitudinal Study (B&B) examines education and work experiences after bachelor's degree completion, with particular emphasis on new elementary and secondary teachers, tracking cohorts at one, four, and ten years post-graduation. Four cohorts have been followed, with the most recent completing degrees in 2015–16; the study collects data on workforce participation, earnings, graduate school enrollment, student loan debt, homeownership, and teaching careers. Recent findings show that among 2015–16 graduates, 41% pursued additional education within four years, 74% worked full-time, and significant gender-based salary gaps existed one year after graduation.

---

### 424. Schools and Staffing Survey (SASS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, professional-development, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/sass/

The Schools and Staffing Survey (SASS) was an integrated national study of public and private school districts, schools, principals, and teachers designed to provide descriptive data on the context of elementary and secondary education. Conducted seven times between 1987 and 2011, SASS gathered data on teacher demand and compensation, principal and teacher characteristics, school climate, hiring and retention practices, and student demographics. The program was supplemented by the Teacher Follow-Up Survey and Principal Follow-Up Survey tracking mobility and attrition, and was subsequently redesigned and relaunched as the National Teacher and Principal Survey in 2015–16.

---

### 425. Private School Universe Survey (PSS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/pss/

The Private School Universe Survey (PSS) generates biennial data on private schools, teachers, and students in the United States, targeting all institutions not primarily supported by public funds that provide classroom instruction for grades K–12 and employ at least one teacher. Collecting data since 1989–90, the survey gathers information on religious orientation, school level and size, enrollment, high school graduates, gender composition, teacher counts, program emphasis, and kindergarten offerings. The PSS produces data comparable to the Common Core of Data for public schools, enabling cross-sector analysis of enrollment trends including growth patterns in religiously-affiliated schools.

---

### 426. School Survey on Crime and Safety (SSOCS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, school-discipline, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/ssocs/

The School Survey on Crime and Safety (SSOCS) is the primary source of school-level data on crime and safety for the U.S. Department of Education, collecting information from approximately 4,800 nationally representative public elementary and secondary schools. The survey covers topics related to school crime, violence, discipline, and safety conditions, with periodic data collection and public-use data files available through NCES DataLab. Recent data releases include 2021–22 school year findings alongside historical data through 2019–20, making SSOCS an essential resource for understanding trends in school safety conditions over time.

---

### 427. High School and Beyond Longitudinal Study (HS&B)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, longitudinal, career-readiness, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/hsb/

The High School and Beyond Longitudinal Study (HS&B) is the sixth in a series of NCES longitudinal studies, originally tracking nationally representative cohorts of 10th and 12th graders from 1980 through multiple follow-up surveys to examine how educational system factors influence students' educational and career outcomes. The study collected student and parent questionnaires, cognitive assessments, and high school and postsecondary transcripts, capturing trajectories from high school into the workforce and postsecondary education. Notable findings include associations between advanced high school coursetaking (Algebra II or higher) and lower unemployment at midlife, and data on young adult living arrangements across cohorts.

---

### 428. National Longitudinal Study of the High School Class of 1972 (NLS-72)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, longitudinal, career-readiness, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/nls72/

The National Longitudinal Study of the High School Class of 1972 (NLS-72) pioneered longitudinal research methodology for examining how high school experiences predict career and educational outcomes, following over 21,000 high school seniors through periodic surveys until 1986, with postsecondary transcripts collected in 1984. The study intentionally oversampled schools serving disadvantaged and minority populations and linked educational experiences with early labor market participation and postsecondary enrollment. Findings include that over 90% of participants engaged in paid work within two years of graduation, and the study established a foundational design replicated in subsequent NCES longitudinal programs.

---

### 429. High School Transcript Studies (HST)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/hst/

The High School Transcript Studies (HST) collect official academic records from high school students to examine coursetaking patterns and predict future educational outcomes, gathering data on courses taken, credits earned, course sequencing, final grades, class rank, and standardized test scores where available. Transcript data were collected in conjunction with multiple NCES longitudinal studies (HS&B, NELS:88, ELS:2002, HSLS:09) and the National Assessment of Educational Progress (NAEP), spanning collection years from 1982 to 2019. All data are classified using the standardized six-digit Classification of Secondary School Courses coding system and released only as restricted-use files to licensed researchers to protect student confidentiality.

---

### 430. ED School Climate Surveys (EDSCLS)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, sel, formative-assessment, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/edscls/

The ED School Climate Surveys (EDSCLS) provide a suite of nationally available survey instruments developed by NCES to measure school climate from multiple stakeholder perspectives, including students, teachers, non-instructional staff, principals, and parents or guardians. The surveys assess school environment across three domains and 13 topics, with a platform enabling schools, districts, and states to collect and report comparable climate data at the local level. NCES has developed psychometric benchmarks supporting meaningful comparisons across student subgroups and institutions, with scores generated at school, district, and state levels.

---

### 431. Education Finance Statistics Center (EDFIN)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/edfin/

The Education Finance Statistics Center (EDFIN) provides financial information and data on public elementary and secondary education in the United States, collecting annual revenues and expenditures data for public schools and school districts alongside fiscal and nonfiscal trend information. The center offers interactive data tools enabling district-level comparisons, the NCES Financial Handbook, and annual publications on education revenues and expenditures by fiscal year. EDFIN serves as the primary federal source for tracking how public education is funded and where resources are allocated across the nation's school districts.

---

### 432. Statewide Longitudinal Data Systems (SLDS) Grant Program

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, longitudinal, data-sharing, pii-privacy, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/programs/slds/

The Statewide Longitudinal Data Systems (SLDS) Grant Program supports states in designing, developing, implementing, and expanding K-12 and P-20W (early learning through the workforce) longitudinal data systems that enable evidence-based decision-making across educational levels. The program provides grants, technical assistance, publications, webinars, and a State Support Team to help state education agencies build data infrastructure that tracks student progress from early childhood into the workforce. Key resources include best practices guides, a Research Request Process Toolkit, school-level poverty measures, and connections to federal initiatives such as Common Education Data Standards.

---

### 433. Library Statistics Program

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/libraries/

The Library Statistics Program collects and distributes statistical data on libraries across the U.S. education system, covering academic libraries, public libraries, state library agencies, and elementary/secondary school library media centers. The academic library component was reintegrated into the IPEDS collection as a mandatory annual survey, with data from 2014 onward accessible through the IPEDS Use the Data portal and historical data from 1996–2012 available through dedicated files. The program maintains historical records extending back to 1989 for public libraries, enabling long-term trend analysis of library resources, staffing, and usage across institutional types.

---

### 434. International Activities Program (IAP)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/international/

The International Activities Program (IAP) coordinates U.S. participation in large-scale international education studies and assessments to make comparative data available on education and learning across nations. The program administers seven current international studies—including PIRLS, TIMSS, ICILS, PISA, TALIS, PIAAC, and IELS—covering mathematics, science, reading, financial literacy, problem-solving, computer literacy, and adult skills in literacy and numeracy for populations ranging from early childhood through adults aged 16–65. Results typically release 18–24 months after data collection and inform U.S. education policy by contextualizing American student and adult performance within global education systems.

---

### 435. Education Across America: Cities, Suburbs, Towns, and Rural Areas (Locale Studies)

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, early-childhood, higher-ed, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/annualreports/topical-studies/locale

The NCES locale studies resource hub, "Education Across America: Cities, Suburbs, Towns, and Rural Areas," compiles comparative data for individuals interested in the condition of education across different geographic locales in the United States. The hub provides tabulations, an interactive "At a Glance" data tool, and indicators spanning family characteristics, educational experiences, school resources and staffing, and educational outcomes across urban, suburban, town, and rural communities. Topics covered include early childhood care, college preparatory coursework, teacher staffing, graduation rates, and postsecondary enrollment, enabling researchers and policymakers to identify geographic disparities in educational opportunity.

---

### 436. Current Population Survey (CPS) — Education Supplements

Type: dataset | Source: National Center for Education Statistics (NCES)
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, early-childhood, english-learners, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/cps/

The Current Population Survey (CPS) is a monthly household survey of approximately 50,000–60,000 dwelling units conducted by the Bureau of the Census for the Bureau of Labor Statistics, with NCES funding educational supplements since the late 1960s to provide annual data on school enrollment and educational attainment. The survey's October Supplement gathers school enrollment data across elementary, secondary, and postsecondary levels, plus preschool participation, with supplementary items covering language proficiency, disabilities, computer use and access, student mobility, and private school tuition. The CPS employs a multistage stratified sampling scheme with households rotating in-sample for four months, out for eight, and back for four more, producing nationally representative estimates of the civilian noninstitutionalized population.

---

### 437. International Civic and Citizenship Education Study (ICCS)

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: k-12, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://www.iea.nl/studies/iea/iccs

ICCS is the largest international study dedicated to civic and citizenship education, assessing Grade 8 students' civic knowledge, beliefs, attitudes, and behaviors related to democratic participation. The study also collects contextual data on curriculum, teaching practices, and school climate, with cycles in 2009, 2016, and 2022, and a fully digital 2027 cycle in progress. ICCS data serve as the primary evidence source for UN Sustainable Development Goal indicator 4.7.4 on global citizenship understanding.

---

### 438. International Computer and Information Literacy Study (ICILS)

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: k-12, digital-learning-platforms, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://www.iea.nl/studies/iea/icils

ICILS measures how well Grade 8 students across multiple educational systems are prepared for study, work, and life in a digital world, assessing computer and information literacy (CIL) including the knowledge and skills needed to use technology for investigation, creation, and communication. The study has run in 2013, 2018, and 2023 cycles, with a 2028 cycle currently underway, and supports monitoring of UN SDG targets and EU education priorities. Contextual data on students' home and school technology environments are collected alongside achievement scores.

---

### 439. Teacher Education and Development Study in Mathematics (TEDS-M)

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: math-education, professional-development, open-datasets
URL: https://www.iea.nl/data-tools/repository/tedsm

TEDS-M examined teacher education programs and their role in developing mathematics instruction capacity, with data collection conducted in 2007-08 across 17 countries. The dataset is maintained by the IEA Research and Analysis Unit and remains publicly available for researcher access upon completion of a nondisclosure and user agreement, given the sensitive nature of participant data. The study is citable via DOI (https://doi.org/10.58150/IEA_TEDS-M_2008) and is actively used in teacher education research; documentation is available through the User Guide for the TEDS-M 2008 International Database.

---

### 440. Responses to Educational Disruption Survey (REDS)

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: k-12, longitudinal, open-datasets
URL: https://www.iea.nl/data-tools/repository/REDS

REDS examined the impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on lower secondary education (Grade 8) across 11 nations including Burkina Faso, Denmark, Ethiopia, India, Kenya, Rwanda, Slovenia, the UAE, Uruguay, and Uzbekistan, with data collected between December 2020 and July 2021. The survey gathered internationally comparable responses from 21,063 students, 15,004 teachers, and 1,581 school principals, enabling cross-national analysis of pandemic-related educational disruption. The dataset is available in SAS and SPSS formats through the IEA Data Repository and is citable via DOI (https://doi.org/10.58150/REDS_2021_data).

---

### 441. College Scorecard Data

Type: dataset | Source: U.S. Department of Education
Tags: higher-ed, longitudinal, college-access, open-datasets
URL: https://collegescorecard.ed.gov/data/

College Scorecard Data provides downloadable institution-level files for 1996-97 through 2022-23 containing aggregate data on institutional characteristics, enrollment, student aid, costs, and student outcomes, plus field-of-study-level files covering cumulative debt at graduation and earnings one year after graduation. The dataset is updated periodically (last updated March 23, 2026) and also accessible via a public REST API with documentation available on the same site. Crosswalk files link the Department's OPEID identifiers with IPEDS UNITIDs, enabling integration with other federal higher education data sources.

---

### 442. Education Stabilization Fund (ESF) COVID-19 Relief Data

Type: dataset | Source: U.S. Department of Education
Tags: k-12, higher-ed, open-datasets
URL: https://covid-relief-data.ed.gov

The Education Stabilization Fund data portal tracks over $276 billion in federal COVID-19 education relief awarded across four programs: Elementary and Secondary School Emergency Relief (ESSER, $189.5B), Higher Education Emergency Relief (HEER, $75.2B), Emergency Assistance to Non-Public Schools (EANS, $5.5B), and Governor's Emergency Education Relief (GEER, $4.3B). The portal provides grantee-level expenditure data searchable by state, district, and institution, with bulk downloads of annual performance report datasets and a public API. Data covers over 16,000 school districts and 4,500 colleges and universities through the reporting period ending January 2026.

---

### 443. ASSISTments 2012-13 School Data with Affect

Type: dataset | Source: Worcester Polytechnic Institute
Tags: open-datasets, k-12, learning-engineering, assistments, wpi, intelligent-tutoring, computer-assisted-learning, formative-assessment, digital-learning-platforms
URL: https://sites.google.com/site/assistmentsdata/datasets/2012-13-school-data-with-affect

A large-scale log of approximately 10 million student problem-solving interactions from the ASSISTments intelligent tutoring system during the 2012-2013 school year, augmented with machine-learning predictions of four affective states per interaction — frustration, confusion, engagement/concentration, and boredom — scored on a 0-to-1 scale. Records include student attempts, hint requests, response times, problem metadata, skill tags, and classroom/school identifiers, enabling research on the relationship between student affect and math learning outcomes in K-12 settings.

---

### 444. ASSISTments Skill-Builder Data 2009-2010

Type: dataset | Source: Worcester Polytechnic Institute
Tags: open-datasets, k-12, learning-engineering, assistments, wpi, intelligent-tutoring, computer-assisted-learning, formative-assessment, math-education
URL: https://sites.google.com/site/assistmentsdata/home/2009-2010-assistment-data/skill-builder-data-2009-2010

Student interaction logs from ASSISTments skill-builder problem sets used in K-12 mathematics during the 2009-2010 school year, structured as one row per student-problem attempt. Each skill-builder focuses on a single mathematics skill (with optional multi-skill tagging) and requires students to answer three consecutive questions correctly before moving on; the dataset captures correctness, hint usage, and response sequences under this mastery criterion. A corrected, deduplicated version is available via Google Drive alongside the original CSV.

---

### 445. Literacy and Numeracy Assessment (LaNA)

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: open-datasets, k-12, literacy, math-education, early-childhood
URL: https://www.iea.nl/studies/iea/LaNA

LaNA is an international assessment of emerging mathematics and reading comprehension skills at the end of primary school (grades 4–6 depending on context), designed for countries that need timely, reliable, nationally representative, and internationally comparable education data. It is grounded in and linked to TIMSS and PIRLS, using the same benchmarks to track progress toward SDG Indicator 4.1.1b. The study collects contextual information about resources, learning experiences, and school environments alongside achievement data. Six countries have administered LaNA: Burkina Faso, Egypt, Nigeria, Pakistan, Palestinian National Authority, and Senegal, with earlier pilots in Haiti, North Macedonia, Punjab (Pakistan), and Serbia. Initial administrations occurred in 2016–2020 (pilots) and 2023 (linking study).

---

### 446. TIMSS Advanced

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: open-datasets, k-12, math-education, longitudinal
URL: https://www.iea.nl/data-tools/repository/timssadvanced

TIMSS Advanced assesses students in their final year of secondary school who are enrolled in advanced mathematics and physics programs. It is the only international assessment measuring student readiness for university-level STEM studies, gathering policy-relevant data on curriculum emphasis, technology use, and teacher preparation to support education reform and STEM policy planning. Data from three cycles are available through the IEA repository in SAS and SPSS formats: 1995, 2008, and 2015. Each dataset is assigned a DOI for citation purposes.

---

### 447. TIMSS Longitudinal

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: open-datasets, k-12, math-education, longitudinal
URL: https://www.iea.nl/data-tools/repository/timsslongitudinal

TIMSS Longitudinal is an optional extension of TIMSS 2023 that measures student learning gains over one year of schooling by assessing the same cohort at two points in time. It targets students in grades 4–5 and grades 8–9, capturing growth in mathematics and science achievement across a critical schooling period. Data from the 2023 and 2024 collections are publicly available in SAS, SPSS, and R formats through the IEA data repository, with DOI citations provided for academic use.

---

### 448. CIVED — Civic Education Study

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: open-datasets, k-12
URL: https://www.iea.nl/data-tools/repository/cived

CIVED was an international assessment covering the content domains of democracy and citizenship, national identity, and social cohesion and diversity. Described as the largest and most rigorous study of civic education conducted internationally at the time, it assessed students at grades 8 and 12. Phase 1 of the study ran from 1996–1997 and Phase 2 from 1999–2000. Datasets for the 1999 assessment cycles at both grade levels are publicly available in SAS and SPSS formats through the IEA data repository. CIVED is the predecessor to ICCS, which continues civic education measurement in subsequent cycles.

---

### 449. IELS — International Early Learning and Child Well-being Study

Type: dataset | Source: IEA
Tags: open-datasets, early-childhood
URL: https://www.iea.nl/studies/additional/IELS

IELS is the first international large-scale assessment focused on five-year-old children, examining early learning, home background and learning environments, and experiences in early childhood education. It measures both cognitive domains (emergent numeracy and literacy) and non-cognitive domains (self-regulation and empathy) through tablet-based one-to-one sessions with audio recordings. The first cycle was completed in 2018 in three countries; a second cycle, IELS 2024, is currently underway. The study is coordinated by the OECD Secretariat with a consortium led by the Australian Council for Educational Research, including IEA and cApStAn as partners.

---

### 450. Duolingo Student Learning Traces (Spaced Repetition / Half-Life Regression)

Type: dataset | Source: Duolingo
Tags: open-datasets, learning-engineering, nlp, duolingo, english-learners, longitudinal, computer-assisted-learning, digital-learning-platforms
URL: https://dataverse.harvard.edu/dataset.xhtml?persistentId=doi:10.7910/DVN/N8XJME

A dataset of 13 million student learning traces from Duolingo, capturing vocabulary practice sessions across multiple language pairs. Released alongside the paper "A Trainable Spaced Repetition Model for Language Learning" (Settles & Meeder, ACL 2016), which introduced the half-life regression algorithm for modeling memory decay. Each record represents a single lesson or practice session and includes recall accuracy, timing, student and language identifiers, and word-level history of exposures and correct answers (12 columns total). The dataset is available as a 361 MB gzipped CSV and is hosted on Harvard Dataverse. Code is available at https://github.com/duolingo/halflife-regression. Descriptions sourced from research.duolingo.com and the GitHub repository README.

---

### 451. STEP Skills Measurement Program

Type: dataset | Source: World Bank
Tags: open-datasets, higher-ed
URL: https://microdata.worldbank.org/index.php/catalog/step

The STEP (Skills Toward Employment and Productivity) Skills Measurement Program is the World Bank's first initiative to generate internationally comparable data on workforce skills in low- and middle-income countries. The program administers household and employer surveys across 17 countries — including Armenia, Bolivia, Colombia, Georgia, Ghana, Kenya, and Vietnam — measuring cognitive skills (reading, writing, numeracy), socio-emotional competencies, and job-specific skills, along with education and training histories. The collection of 22 studies is publicly available through the World Bank Microdata Library, with each country survey including a direct reading literacy assessment based on the Programme for the International Assessment of Adult Competencies (PIAAC) instruments.

---

### 452. Service Delivery Indicators Education Survey 2014 — Tanzania

Type: dataset | Source: World Bank
Tags: open-datasets, k-12
URL: https://microdata.worldbank.org/index.php/catalog/2748

This World Bank dataset examines primary education service delivery quality across Tanzania through a 2014 survey of 400 primary schools. It captures three standardized indicator categories: teacher effort (school and classroom absence rates, daily teaching time), teacher knowledge (subject matter competency in English, mathematics, and pedagogy), and availability of inputs (infrastructure, textbooks, equipment, and pupil-teacher ratios). The dataset also includes direct grade-4 student assessments in language, mathematics, and non-verbal reasoning, and is harmonized to enable cross-country comparisons within the broader Service Delivery Indicators initiative covering Sub-Saharan Africa.

---

### 453. National Longitudinal Study of Adolescent to Adult Health (Add Health), 1994–2025

Type: dataset | Source: ICPSR (U. Michigan)
Tags: open-datasets, k-12, higher-ed, longitudinal
URL: https://www.icpsr.umich.edu/web/ICPSR/studies/21600

Add Health is a nationally representative longitudinal panel study tracking a cohort of U.S. adolescents from grades 7–12 (1994–95) through early midlife, with data collection across six waves extending to 2025 when participants were ages 39–51. The study combines survey data on social, economic, psychological, and physical well-being with rich contextual information on families, schools, neighborhoods, and peer and romantic relationships; later waves add biospecimens, physical measurements, and comprehensive life history data. It is one of the largest and most widely cited longitudinal datasets in U.S. education and adolescent development research, supporting studies of school transitions, educational attainment, and long-term health and socioeconomic outcomes.

---

### 454. WPI — ASSISTments Math 2004–2005 (912 Students)

Type: dataset | Source: Carnegie Mellon University LearnLab
Tags: open-datasets, learning-engineering, math-education, k-12, intelligent-tutoring, assistments, cmu-learnlab
URL: https://pslcdatashop.web.cmu.edu/DatasetInfo?datasetId=92

A public dataset in the PSLC DataShop repository containing interaction logs from 912 students using the ASSISTments intelligent tutoring system during the 2004–2005 academic year. The dataset, contributed by PI Neil Heffernan (Worcester Polytechnic Institute), records student problem-solving transactions in middle-school mathematics. It is one of three ASSISTments datasets in DataShop spanning 2004–2007, with this cohort containing approximately 580,785 transactions. Part of the WPI–ASSISTments project (DataShop ID 92), listed as a public project accessible to registered DataShop users.

---

### 455. WPI — ASSISTments Math 2005–2006 (3136 Students)

Type: dataset | Source: Carnegie Mellon University LearnLab
Tags: open-datasets, learning-engineering, math-education, k-12, intelligent-tutoring, assistments, cmu-learnlab
URL: https://pslcdatashop.web.cmu.edu/DatasetInfo?datasetId=120

A public PSLC DataShop dataset capturing 3,136 students' interactions with the ASSISTments intelligent tutoring platform during the 2005–2006 school year, contributed by PI Neil Heffernan. ASSISTments provides students with scaffolded math problem-solving practice while simultaneously collecting fine-grained transaction-level data (student responses, hints requested, errors made) suitable for knowledge component modeling and learning curve analysis. This dataset (DataShop ID 120) contains approximately 1,451,003 transactions — the largest of the three ASSISTments cohorts in DataShop. Listed as a public project on the DataShop catalog.

### 456. Geometry Area (1996–97)

Type: dataset | Source: Carnegie Mellon University LearnLab
Tags: open-datasets, learning-engineering, math-education, k-12, intelligent-tutoring, cmu-learnlab
URL: https://pslcdatashop.web.cmu.edu/DatasetInfo?datasetId=76

One of the oldest and most widely used benchmark datasets in educational data mining, this public PSLC DataShop dataset records students' interactions with a Geometry Area Cognitive Tutor during the 1996–97 academic year. PI Ken Koedinger (CMU). The dataset has been assigned a persistent DOI (10.60710/DATASET-76) as part of DataShop's April 2026 DOI release. It has been used in numerous learning science and EDM studies and was featured as the standard teaching dataset for the EDM Summer School 2017 (DataShop ID 2174). Subject area: Math/Geometry. Listed as a public project.

### 457. Physics Course — Andes2 (USNA, 2005–2010)

Type: dataset | Source: Carnegie Mellon University LearnLab
Tags: open-datasets, learning-engineering, higher-ed, intelligent-tutoring, computer-assisted-learning, cmu-learnlab
URL: https://pslcdatashop.web.cmu.edu/DatasetInfo?datasetId=126

A public collection of 15 datasets capturing physics students' problem-solving interactions with the Andes2 intelligent tutoring system, contributed by PI Kurt VanLehn. Data spans multiple institutions and semesters from 2001 to 2010, primarily at the United States Naval Academy (USNA) but also including Watchung Hills Regional High School, St. Anselm College, and others. Individual datasets range from roughly 10,000 to 345,000 transactions. Andes is a physics tutor that provides step-by-step problem-solving support with hints and error feedback. The dataset collection (DataShop IDs 126, 157, 220, 233–238, 263, 265, 267, 302–304, 408–412) is listed as a public project on DataShop.

### 458. Junyi Academy Math Practicing Log (to January 2015)

Type: dataset | Source: Carnegie Mellon University LearnLab
Tags: open-datasets, learning-engineering, math-education, k-12, digital-learning-platforms, personalized-learning, cmu-learnlab
URL: https://pslcdatashop.web.cmu.edu/DatasetInfo?datasetId=1198

A public PSLC DataShop dataset contributed by PI Haw-Shiuan Chang capturing student math practice logs from Junyi Academy, a Taiwanese e-learning platform described as functionally similar to Khan Academy. The dataset records student interactions with mathematics exercises through January 2015 and is available in full (DataShop ID 1198) and partial-sample (DataShop ID 1275) versions. Subject area: Math/Other. Listed as a public project, this large-scale log dataset from a deployed online platform is suited for studies of learning trajectories, knowledge component modeling, and engagement in self-paced digital learning environments.
